## Top 50 Must-Know Platforms
1. GitHub - Code hosting and collaboration.
2. VS Code - Most popular code editor.
3. Stack Overflow - Developer Q&A community.
4. Google Cloud Platform - Cloud infrastructure.
5. AWS - Cloud infrastructure.
6. Azure - Cloud infrastructure.
7. Vercel - Frontend deployment platform.
8. Netlify - Frontend deployment platform.
9. Figma - Design and prototyping.
10. Notion - All-in-one workspace.
11. ChatGPT - AI assistant.
12. Claude - AI assistant.
13. Stripe - Payment processing.
14. Firebase - Backend as a service.
15. Supabase - Open source Firebase alternative.
16. Docker - Containerization platform.
17. Kubernetes - Container orchestration.
18. Postman - API development and testing.
19. MongoDB - NoSQL database.
20. PostgreSQL - Relational database.
21. Redis - In-memory data store.
22. Slack - Team communication.
23. Discord - Community and team communication.
24. Trello - Project management.
25. Jira - Agile project management.
26. npm - JavaScript package manager.
27. PyPI - Python package manager.
28. Docker Hub - Container registry.
29. Canva - Simple design tool.
30. Webflow - No-code website builder.
31. Airtable - No-code database.
32. Zapier - Automation platform.
33. Heroku - PaaS platform.
34. DigitalOcean - Cloud hosting.
35. Cloudflare - CDN and security.
36. Sentry - Error tracking and monitoring.
37. Datadog - Monitoring and analytics.
38. New Relic - Observability platform.
39. Twilio - Communication APIs.
40. Mailchimp - Email marketing.
41. SendGrid - Email delivery.
42. Algolia - Search API.
43. Auth0 - Authentication and authorization.
44. Clerk - Authentication for React.
45. PlanetScale - Serverless MySQL database.
46. Upstash - Serverless Redis and Kafka.
47. Railway - Infrastructure platform.
48. Fly.io - Edge computing platform.
49. Render - Cloud hosting.
50. Framer - Interactive design and prototyping.
